	}

 did not match expectation:

	{
	  "method" : "HEAD",
	  "path" : "/foo"
	}

	method matches = false
	path matches = true
	query string parameters match = true
	body matches = true
	headers match = true
	cookies match = true
	keep-alive matches = true
	ssl matches = true
